***раздумывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздумывать.html>разду́мывать</a> (5849)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздумывать.html>разду́мывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razdúmyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздумать.html>разду́мать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to think <i>(about)</i>, to muse <i>(over)</i>, to ponder <i>(over)</i>, to consider, to ruminate <i>(on)</i>, to brood <i>(over)</i>, to deliberate</li>
<li>to hesitate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздумывать.html>разду́мывая</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>razdúmyvaja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">without hesitation; without a moment's thought</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздумье.html>разду́мье</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razdúmʹje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздумывать.html>разду́мывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razdúmyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздумать.html>разду́мать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to change one's mind</li></ol>

***раздуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздуть.html>разду́ть</a> (15984)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>дуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздуть.html>разду́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razdútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздувать.html>раздува́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fan, to blow</li>
<li>to inflate, to blow <i>(out)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to swell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раздуть.html>разду́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёку</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>razdúlo</b> licó (ščóku)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his face (cheek) is swollen</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blow up, to exaggerate</li>
<li>to fan, to boost</li>
<li>to blow about, to flutter</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздуться.html>разду́ться</a> (19027)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздуть.html>разду́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razdútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздуться.html>разду́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razdútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздуваться.html>раздува́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to swell up</li>
<li>to bulge</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздуть.html>разду́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razdútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разинуть.html>рази́нув</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рота.html>рот</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razínuv rot</i> ― <span class="e-translation">agape; open-mouthed</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***разжать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разжать.html>разжа́ть</a> (11197)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разжать.html>разжа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разжимать.html>разжима́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to undo, to open, to unclench, to let down, to release
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разжать.html>разжа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razžátʹ</b> ruki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unclasp one's hands</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***разжечь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разжечь.html>разже́чь</a> (13352)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жечь.html>жечь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разжечь.html>разже́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razžéčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разжигать.html>разжига́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to light, to kindle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разжечь.html>разже́чь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрова.html>дрова́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>ого́нь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razžéčʹ</b> drová ogónʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to kindle the firewood [fire]</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to inflame, to stir up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rouse</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***разжигать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разжигать.html>разжига́ть</a> (13434)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-жига́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-žigátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разжигать.html>разжига́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razžigátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разжечь.html>разже́чь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to light, to kindle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разжигать.html>разжига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрова.html>дрова́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>ого́нь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razžigátʹ</b> drová ogónʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to kindle the firewood [fire]</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to inflame, to stir up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разжигать.html>разжига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ненависть.html>не́нависть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razžigátʹ</b> nénavistʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stir up [foment] hatred</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разжигать.html>разжига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:любовь.html>любо́вь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razžigátʹ</b> ljubóvʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to kindle the flame of love; kindle love into a flame</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разжигать.html>разжига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:страсть.html>стра́сти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razžigátʹ</b> strásti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to inflame the passions; arouse passion</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разжигать.html>разжига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:национальный.html>национа́льную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вражда.html>вражду́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razžigátʹ</b> nacionálʹnuju vraždú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rouse [stir up] national hatred</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rouse</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***разжимать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разжимать.html>разжима́ть</a> (18142)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-жима́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-žimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разжимать.html>разжима́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razžimátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разжать.html>разжа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to undo, to open, to unclench, to let down, to release
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разжимать.html>разжима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razžimátʹ</b> ruki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unclasp one's hands</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разжимать.html>разжима́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>гу́б</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>razžimája</b> gub</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to without opening one's lips</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разжиматься.html>разжима́ться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razžimátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разжаться.html>разжа́ться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razžátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***разжиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разжиться.html>разжи́ться</a> (19620)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разжиться.html>разжи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razžítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разжива́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get rich, to cash in</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get, to obtain <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental, something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***разинуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разинуть.html>рази́нуть</a> (8747)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orzzinǫti</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orz-</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zinǫti</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">разіну́ць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razinúcʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">razinuti</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">раззи́на</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razzína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Macedonian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Macedonian language">Macedonian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="mk">раззине</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razzine</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разинуть.html>рази́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razínutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разевать.html>разева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to open <i>(wide)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разинуть.html>рази́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рота.html>рот</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razínutʹ</b> rot</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) open wide one's mouth; 2) gape</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разинуть.html>рази́нув</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рота.html>рот</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razínuv</b> rot</i> ― <span class="e-translation">agape; open-mouthed</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">раззя́ва</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razzjáva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">рази́ня</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razínja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***разить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разить.html>рази́ть</a> (12449)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*raziti</i>. Cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резать.html>ре́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разить.html>рази́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сразить.html>срази́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to strike, to hit, to smite</li>
<li>to strike down, to defeat, to crush</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reek (of), to stink (of)</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлагаться.html>разлага́вшийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razlagávšijsja</span>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лага́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lagátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлагать.html>разлага́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razlagátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разложить.html>разложи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to decompose, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to factorize, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(force)</i> to resolve
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разлагать.html>разлага́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>во́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кислород.html>кислоро́д</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:водород.html>водоро́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razlagátʹ</b> vódu na kisloród i vodoród</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to decompose/break water into oxygen and hydrogen</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разлагать.html>разлага́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>число́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> мно́жители</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razlagátʹ</b> čisló na mnóžiteli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to factorize a number</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to demoralize, to corrupt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разлагать.html>разлага́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:армия.html>а́рмию</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razlagátʹ</b> ármiju protívnika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to demoralize/corrupt the enemy's army</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разлагаться.html>разлага́ться</a> (21127)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлагать.html>разлага́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razlagátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлагаться.html>разлага́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razlagátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разложиться.html>разложи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to decompose, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be factorized</li>

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлагать.html>разлага́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razlagátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
